## Embedded Files
26295ee475c715e23255c8616f08f34585f70d45: $$(2+i)z^2+(1-3i)z+(5+i)=0$$

3ad3a917d4c33b5f753def495b65b673c1c72fcb: $$\begin{flalign}
&(2+i)z^2+(1-3i)z+(-5-i)=0 & \\
&\begin{split}
\\D &= (1-3i)^2+4(5+i)(2+i)\\
&=1-6i-9+4(10+7i-1) = -8-6i+36+28i\\
&=28+22i
\end{split}\\\\
&\begin{split}
&\text{найдём }\sqrt{D}:\\&a+bi=\sqrt{28+22i}\\&(a+bi)^2=28+22i\\&a^2-b^2+2abi=28+22i\\
&\begin{cases}
a^2+b^2=28 \\
2ab=22
\end{cases}\\
\end{split}
\end{flalign}$$
